 (define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )

(define (domain house-exploration)

  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )
  
  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )
)


This is previous problem file:

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )
  
  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )
)

(define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )
  
  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )
)

  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )
)

(define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )
)


This is previous problem file: 
(define (problem explore-15)
  (:domain house-exploration)
  (:objects
    kitchen pantry living-room - location
    east west north - direction
  )
  (:init
    (at kitchen)
    (door kitchen pantry east)
    (door pantry kitchen west)
    (door-open kitchen pantry)
    (door-open pantry kitchen)
    (door kitchen living-room north)
    (door living-room kitchen south)
    ; The door between kitchen and living-room is unobserved state (not explicitly open),
    ; so we neither claim open nor closed
  )
  (:goal
    (at living-room)
  )
)

  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)

    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))

(define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )
)

 (define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )
)
 
 (define (problem explore-16)
  (:domain house-exploration)
  (:objects
    kitchen pantry living-room - location
    east west north - direction
  )
  (:init
    (at pantry)
    (door kitchen pantry east)
    (door pantry kitchen west)
    (door-open kitchen pantry)
    (door-open pantry kitchen)
    (door kitchen living-room north)
    (door-closed kitchen living-room)
  )
  (:goal
    (at living-room)
  )
)

(define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
    (unvisited ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)) (not (unvisited ?to)))
  )
)

(define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
    (unvisited ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)) (not (unvisited ?to)))
  )
)

 (define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 - location)
    (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 - location)
    (unvisited ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)) (not (unvisited ?to)))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 - location)
    (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 - location)
    (unvisited ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)) (not (unvisited ?to)))
  )
)

(define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 - location)
    (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 - location)
    (unvisited ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)) (not (unvisited ?to)))
  )
)

  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 - location)
    (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 - location)
    (unvisited ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)) (not (unvisited ?to)))
  )
)


This is previous problem file: 
(define (problem explore-house)
  (:domain house-exploration)
  (:objects
    kitchen pantry living-room - location
    east west north - direction
  )
  (:init
    (at pantry)
    (door kitchen pantry east)
    (door pantry kitchen west)
    (door-open kitchen pantry)
    (door-open pantry kitchen)
    (door kitchen living-room north)
    (door-closed kitchen living-room)
    (unvisited living-room)
    (unvisited kitchen)
  )
  (:goal (at living-room))
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 - location)
    (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 - location)
    (unvisited ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)) (not (unvisited ?to)))
  )
)


This is previous problem file: 
(define (problem explore-house)
  (:domain house-exploration)
  (:objects
    kitchen pantry living-room - location
    east west north - direction
  )
  (:init
    (at pantry)
    (door kitchen pantry east)
    (door pantry kitchen west)
    (door-open kitchen pantry)
    (door-open pantry kitchen)
    (unvisited living-room)
    (door kitchen living-room north)
    (door-closed kitchen living-room)
  )
  (:goal (at living-room))
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 - location)
    (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 - location)
    (unvisited ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)) (not (unvisited ?to)))
  )
)

 (define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 - location)
    (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 - location)
    (unvisited ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)) (not (unvisited ?to)))
  )
)

(define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 - location)
    (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 - location)
    (unvisited ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)) (not (unvisited ?to)))
  )
)

(define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 - location)
    (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 - location)
    (unvisited ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)

    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)) (not (unvisited ?to)))
  )
)

(define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 - location)
    (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 - location)
    (unvisited ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)) (not (unvisited ?to)))
  )
)

(define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 - location)
    (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 - location)
    (unvisited ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)) (not (unvisited ?to)))
  )
)


This is previous problem file: 
(define (problem explore-house)
  (:domain house-exploration)
  (:objects
    kitchen pantry living-room - location
    east west north - direction
  )
  (:init
    (at pantry)
    (door kitchen pantry east)
    (door pantry kitchen west)
    (door-open kitchen pantry)
    (door-open pantry kitchen)
    (door kitchen living-room north)
    (unvisited living-room)
    (unvisited kitchen)
  )
  (:goal (or (at living-room) (at kitchen)))
)

 (define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 - location)
    (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 - location)
    (unvisited ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)) (not (unvisited ?to)))
  )
) 
 (define (problem explore-house)
  (:domain house-exploration)
  (:objects
    kitchen pantry living-room - location
    east west north - direction
  )
  (:init
    (at kitchen)
    (door kitchen pantry east)
    (door pantry kitchen west)
    (door-open kitchen pantry)
    (door-open pantry kitchen)
    (door kitchen living-room north)
    (unvisited living-room)
    (door-closed kitchen living-room)
  )
  (:goal (at living-room))
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 - location)
    (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 - location)
    (unvisited ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)) (not (unvisited ?to)))
  )
)

This is previous problem file:

  (:objects

    (door kitchen living-room north)
    (unvisited living-room)
    (door-closed kitchen living-room)
  )
  (:goal (at living-room))

 (define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 - location)
    (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 - location)
    (unvisited ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)) (not (unvisited ?to)))
  )
)
